DECREE ON THE IMPLEMENTATION OF THE STATE POLICY ON WOMEN IN 
THE REPUBLIC OF AZERBAIJAN 
The Azerbaijani women, with their will, purity and devotion have always played an important 
role in our society and in the formation of our moral values. Our folklore has many positive female 
characters.
The female characters of the epos of «Kitabi-Dede Korkut», the foundation of our moral 
values, is still contributing to the universal values. Our poets praised women as the source of 
life and symbol of wisdom. Our great poet Nizami created such female characters as Mehinbanu, 
Nushabe, Fitna and the seven princesses. The Momina Khatun tomb erected by the prominent 
architect Adjami proves the respect of our people to women. 
The activity of the medieval women of Azerbaijan maintained and enrichened our national 
traditions. The poems by prominent poetess of the 12th century Mehseti Ganjavi won recognition 
abroad. 
Gizil Arslan`s wife Gatiba khanum, Ozbek khan`s wife Mehrjan khanum, Uzun Hasan`s mother 
Sara Khatun, Shah Ismail Khatai`s daughter Mehinbanu, Shirvanshah Khalilullah`s wife Pari 
khanum, Shah Abbas` mother Kheyransa Beyim, legendary Tutu Bike are among the prominent 
stateswomen of the medieval Azerbaijan. 
The 19th century is characterized by the activity and successes of women in Azerbaijan. The 
activity of Khurshud Banu Natavan, Aga Beyim Aga (Agabaji), Gonchabeyim, Fatma khanum 
Kemine, Shahnigar khanum, Gamarbeyim Sheyda Garabagi are much remarkable. The political, 
economic and cultural processes ongoing in Azerbaijan in the 19th century gave an incentive to 
the women become literate and take an active part in the public life. 
Establishment of the secular theatre, democratic press, schools, especially schools for females 
opened new opportunities for the development of the Azerbaijani women. Charity was also popular 
then along enlightenment. Charitable societies established by Govhar khanum Gajar, Hamida 
khanum Javanshir, Nigar khanum Shikhlinskaya, Masma khanum Talishinskaya, Saltanat khanum 
Ahmedova played a prominent role in the public life. One of the charitable actions of that time 
was the establishment of Tazapir Mosque by Nabat khanum Ashurbeyli-Rzayeva. Consequently, 
women gained suffrage  for the fi rst time in our history. 
Establishment of the Democratic Republic of Azerbaijan in 1918 allowed our women become 
ADDITIONAL DOCUMENTS
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
227
www.aliyevheritage.org
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
active members of democratic society. The Azerbaijani women gained a lot of achievements, 
became equal with  men during the Soviet regime. 
The fi rst assembly of the Azerbaijani women was held in 1921. The main idea of that assembly 
was the freedom of women. Afterwards, a lot was done to encourage women become literate and 
take an active part in public life. The Institute of Pre-school education for Women established in 
1921 turned into the Female Teacher-training Institute a year later. In 1923 by name of a journal 
the magazine « rq qadını» («Oriental Woman») started to be published, it became a remarkable 
event in the women movement in Azerbaijan. 
The Second World War urged women to get into labor more widely. Men left for the war, women 
substituted them. A lot of women, such as pilots Leyla Mamedbeyova, Zuleykha Seyidmamedova, 
Sona Nuriyeva, ship captain Shovkat Salimova demonstrated courage in the war. These are the 
bright pages of Azerbaijan connected with women. 
The achievements of the Azerbaijani women during the Soviet time prove their talent and 
industriousness. Actresses Merziye Davudova, Fatma Gadri, Hokume Gurbanova, Munevver 
Kalantarli, Barat Shekinskaya, Leyla Bedirbeyli, Nasiba Zeynalova, Shafi ga Mamedova, 
Amalia Panahova, ballet stars Gamar Almas-zade, Leyla Vekilova, Rafi ga Akhundova, popular 
singers Shovkat Mammadova, Hagigat Rzayeva, Shovkat Alekperova, Sara Gadimova, Rubaba 
Muradova, Fatma Mehraliyeva, Tukezban Ismailova, Zeynab Khanlarova, prominent composers 
Agabaji Rzayeva, Shafi ga Akhundova, Firangiz Ali-zade, great paitners Vajiha Samedova, Reyhan 
Topchubashova, Gullu Mustafayeva, Elmira Shahtakhtinskaya, Maral Rahman-zade contributed 
to the development of our national culture. 
Our women-of-letters such as Nigar Rafi beyli, Mirvarid Dilbazi, Madina Gulgun, Hokuma 
Bulluri, Aziza Jafar-zade, Khanumana Alibeyli contributed to the development of the Azerbaijani 
literature. The assemblies of women held in 1957, 1967, and 1972 played an important role in the 
further development of the women`s movement in Azerbaijan. 
Throughout the 20th century the Azerbaijani women achieved a lot. Serious transformations 
took place in the position of women in socity and family. Despite the achievements, the Soviet 
stereotypes did not take into consideration the traditional values. 
The Azerbaijani women took an active part in the movement of independence. They participated 
in the complicated processes ongoing in the republic in 1988. Among the victims of the tragedy of 
January 20 there were women. Reporter Salatin Askerova and doctor Gultakin Askerova are the 
national heroes of Azerbaijan. There are a lot of women among the refugees who had left their 
homes because of the Armenian occupation. The main problems resulting from the war fell on the 
shoulders of women mostly. The Azerbaijani women, however, have always supported peace. 
The fi rst Constitution of Azerbaijan adopted in 1995 confi rmed the equal right of men and women 
and created a legal basis for the active participation of women in public life. Democratization 
helped the establishment of many women organizations. The major goals of those organizations 
are the improvement of the conditions of women, solution of their problems. 
228
www.aliyevheritage.org
More women organizations are being created, the current ones are expanding their networks. 
During the preparation period of the Sixth World Conference of women held in Beijing in 1995 the 
National Committee of Women of Azerbaijan submitted a report to the conference. 
After the conference national conferences were held. On June 30, 1995, Azerbaijan joined 
the UN Convention on the Elimination of All Forms of Discrimination against Women and took 
respective obligations. 
Since the Beijing Conference a lot of work for the implementation of the principles and 
recommendations noted on its documents has been done and reports have been submitted to the 
UN agencies. 
In order to implement into life the state policy on women, the State Committee on the Problems 
of Women was established with to the decree of the President of the Republic of Azerbaijan on 
January 14, 1998.
The statistics show that among 80 heads of executive power of cities and districts there are only 
5 women, and the number of women  in government bodies is very low.  
Legislative acts, decisions and resolutions adopted by the Cabinet of Ministers, by government 
bodies of various levels do not take into account the gender requirements and do not undergo 
expertise.
Since Azerbaijan regained its independence, women have been assigned new tasks. The 
establishment of market economy, formation of civil society, reforms demand the increase of the 
role of women in society. However, the equal rights determined for women are not realized because 
of lack of equal rights in reality. 
The necessity of solution of the problems of women was emphasized in the fi rst assembly of the 
women of Azerbaijan held on September 25, 1998. That conference demonstrated that a lot has to 
be done to increase the role of  women in society. 
In order to ensure equal rights for women with men, particularly representation of women in 
legislation, I resolve:
1. Equal representation of women with men in the administration must be ensured by taking 
into consideration the activity of all the government bodies of the Republic of Azerbaijan.
2. The State Statistics Committee together with the State Committee on Women`s Problems 
shall prepare statistical information on the situation of women in the republic. 
3. The Cabinet of Ministers shall be charged:
- to ensure equal opportunities both for men and women according to the gender policy within 
the economic reforms;
- to prepare and implement into life a program on the employment of refugees and internally 
displaced people;
- to analyze the current legislation and submit proposals on changes and amendments to the 
laws of the Republic of Azerbaijan in order to strengthen  the defence of women.
- to report the President of the Republic of Azerbaijan on the implementation of the decree until 
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
229
www.aliyevheritage.org
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
March 1;
- to solve issues deriving  from This Decree.
Heydar Aliyev,
President of the Republic of Azerbaijan
Baku, March 6, 2000

LAW OF THE REPUBLIC OF AZERBAIJAN ON GENDER EQUALITY*
Article 1. Aim of the Law
The aim of This Law is to remove all the forms of gender discrimination, to create equal 
opportunities for men and women in all the spheres of political, economic, social and cultural life 
by ensuring gender equality.
Article 2. Basic notions
2.0. The following notions are used in This Law:
2.01. Gender- social aspect of relations between men and women in the political, economic, 
cultural and other spheres of public life;
2.02. Gender equality- equality of rights of men and women, equal opportunities for ensuring 
these rights and their equal status in the society;
2.03. Equal opportunities- equal conditions and guarantees for men and women in ensuring 
human rights;
2.04. Sex discrimination- sexual harassment, employment of discrimination which includes 
sexual advances, requests for sexual favours, and other verbal or other physical conduct of a 
sexual nature in the course of employment;
2.05. Sexual harassment- abusive and humiliating actions committed at work and service 
relations, insulting in nature, expressed in physical actions (verbal, by touching, by abusive words, 
gestures, threat, soiling proposals and invitation of immoral nature)
Article 3. Prohibition of all forms of gender discrimination
3.1. All the forms of gender discrimination are prohibited
3.2. The followings are not regarded to be gender discrimination:
3.2.1. Concessions, privileges and other forms of maintenance provided by the Labour Code of 
the Republic of Azerbaijan for women;
3.2.2. Call up of men for the active military (alternative) service;
3.2.3. different pension and marriage ages for men and women as provided by the law;
3.2.4. restriction of the right of the husband to demand the breach of the marriage in conformity 
with Article 15 of the Family Code of the Republic of Azerbaijan;
3.2.5. creation of different conditions for men and women in penitentiaries; 
3.2.6. implementation of special measures into life for ensuring gender equality.
Article 4. Ban of harassment to sexual intercourse
Compulsion to sexual intercourse is prohibited.
Article 5. Basic directions of the national policy connected with the assurance of gender 
equality.
5.0. The basic directions of the national policy for ensuring gender equality are the 
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
* This is not offi cial translation
231
www.aliyevheritage.org
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
followings:
5.0.1. formation, improvement and development of the normative legal base for ensuring 
gender equality;
5.0.2. conduction of gender expertise of the normative legal acts;
5.0.3. development and materialization of national programs for ensuring gender equality;
5.0.4. propagation of the culture of gender equality.
Article 6. Objectives of the state in ensuring gender equality
The state takes measures for removing all the forms of the gender inequality, for creating equal 
opportunities for men and women, for not allowing the representative of one sex have superiority 
on the representative of another sex in the administration of the country, in the adoption of 
decisions.
Article 7. The objectives of the employers
7.1. The employer ensures the equality of men and women at work.
7.2. The employer has the following objectives:
7.2.1. to treat equally and create equal opportunities for anyone in the employment, in the 
promotion at work, in the acquisition of new professions, in the improvement of one’s qualifi cation, 
in the appreciation of one’s work and in cases of dismissal, irrespective of the sex;
7.2.2. to create the same work conditions for persons engaged in the same work, irrespective 
of their sexes;
7.2.3. not to apply different forms of punishment to persons for the same violation of discipline, 
irrespective of their sexes;
7.2.4. to fulfi ll the provisions of Article 9 and Article 10 of This Law;
7.2.5. to take measures for preventing to sexual harassment and discrimination because of 
one’s sex: 
Article 8. The objectives of the employer in removing gender discrimination 
8.1. The employer must substantiate that his decision on employment, promotion at work, 
improvement of one’s qualifi cations, requalifi cation, estimation of the quality of one’s work, 
dismissal from work does not depend on the sex of the employee if there appears a different 
approach in the said. 
8.2. The employee has the right to demand from the employer to give him/her a written 
explanation on the education, professionalism, experience, professional qualities and other 
preferences on the employment of the representative of the opposite sex in the case he/she refused 
of employment.
Article 9. Equality in the payment of labour
9.1. The persons working at the place and position with same professional skills and degrees, in 
the same work conditions must be paid the same wages, rewards and others for the encouragement 
for the work of the same value, irrespective of their sexes. 
9.2. When the wages, rewards and others paid for encouragement for the same work of the same 
232
www.aliyevheritage.org
value differ, at the demand of the employee the employer must substantiate that the differences are 
not connected with the differences in the sexes of the employees. 
Article 10. Announcements with discriminatory contents
10.1. The announcements on employment are not allowed to have different demands for men 
and women, preference to the representative of a defi nite sex, questions about the marital state or 
private life of the job-seeker. 
10.2. It is banned to publish announcements of deceptive content, contradicting the principles 
of gender equality. 
10.3. It is not allowed to announce vacancies only for the representatives of one sex.
10.4. The publication of announcements mentioned in Article 10.3 of the Present Law are 
allowed only in those cases when the sex of the employee is the only decisive condition for 
employment because of the nature of the work, or in conformity with the Labour Code of the 
Republic of Azerbaijan the use of the labour of woman is banned in such jobs. 
Article 11. Inadmissibility of any pressure against the employees subjected to sexual 
harassment
The persons who have complained from the employer, or managers for being subjected to sexual 
harassment can not be subjected to any pressure on the part of the employer or the manager.
Article 12. Annulment of the labour contract
The labour contract of the person subjected to sexual harassment is annulled since the day 
shown in his/her application. 
Article 13. Equal opportunities in the execution of education rights 
13.1. The state ensures equal opportunities for men and women for enjoying their rights to 
education.
13.2. The employer ensures equal opportunities for men and women for getting the fi rst and 
additional educations, for enjoying vacation rights connected with the education. 
13.3. The state ensures equal opportunities for men and women in the admission to the 
educational institutions, in granting scholarships to students, in the selection of curricula and 
in the assessment of the knowledge in all the educational institutions irrespective of their being 
national, or private.
13.4. Text books must ensure the principle of gender equality. 
Article 14. Gender discrimination in the activity of educational institutions
14.0. The following cases can be regarded as cases of gender discrimination in the activity of 
the educational institutions. 
14.0.1. Application of different requirements to men and women in the admission to educational 
institutions, in the development of curricula and in the assessment of their knowledge. 
14.0.2. Creation of different opportunities for men and women in the selection of the sphere of 
education.
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
233
www.aliyevheritage.org
In the Name of the Azerba  ani Woman
Article 15. Assurance of gender equality in economic and social relations
15.1. The state ensures the creation of equal opportunities for men and woman in the execution 
of their property rights, for being engaged in entrepreneurial activities. 
15.2. The state ensures the creation of equal opportunities for men and women in the execution 
of their rights of social maintenance, in getting the addressed social allowances and other social 
concessions from the state.
Article 16. Assurance of gender equality in the activity of political parties, non-governmental 
organizations, trade unions. 
16.1. Affi liation to political parties, non-governmental organizations and trade unions is open 
for men and women on equal conditions, and equal opportunities must be created for both of 
them.
16.2. The provisions of Article 16.1 of This Law are not applied to the activities of the non-
governmental organizations set up for the defence of the interests of a defi nite sex.
Article 17. The right of demanding the payment of damages
17.1. The persons subjected to gender discrimination are paid for the damages in the form as 
provided by the legislation of the Republic of Azerbaijan.
17.2. Persons subjected to sexual harassment are paid damages in the form as provided by the 
legislation of the Republic of Azerbaijan. 
Article 18. Responsibilities for the violation of the law Persons guilty in the violation of the 
provisions of This Law bear responsibility in conformity with the legislation of the Republic of 
Azerbaijan.
Article 19. Control on the assurance of gender equality 
Control on the assurance of gender equality is exercised by a respective body of the executive 
power
Article 20. Annual report of the body of the executive power which controls the assurance of 
the gender equality
The body of the executive power which exercises control on the assurance of gender equality, 
submits its annual report to the parliament of the Republic on its activities.
Article 21. Enforcement of the law 
This Law gains force since the day of its signature. 
Ilham Aliyev 
President of the Republic of Azerbaijan. 
Baku, October 10, 2006.
